</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Reports Fiscal 2024 Second Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Second quarter operational results in line with expectations, U.S. Healthcare achieved adjusted EBITDA profitability, narrowing full-year
adjusted EPS guidance range </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Second quarter financial highlights </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter; Second quarter results included a $5.8&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charge related to VillageMD
goodwill </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

currency basis reflecting lower adjusted effective tax rate** and improved profitability in U.S. Healthcare </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Fiscal 2024 guidance<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> </I></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

U.S., early wind-down of sale-leaseback program, and lower earnings due to Cencora share sales, offset by execution in pharmacy services and a lower adjusted effective tax rate** </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Maintaining U.S. Healthcare adjusted EBITDA** to be breakeven at the midpoint of the guidance range of ($50)
million to $50&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill. &#151; March&nbsp;28, 2024 &#151; Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today
announced financial results for the second quarter of fiscal 2024, which ended February&nbsp;29, 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Chief Executive Officer Tim Wentworth said: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We&#146;re encouraged by our first quarter of U.S. Healthcare positive adjusted EBITDA and continued topline growth alongside another quarter of strong
execution in pharmacy, as we look to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-energize</FONT> and evolve its impact both at Walgreens and at large. As we continue to operate in a challenging retail environment, we are taking actions to focus on customer
engagement and value. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We remain confident in our goal of achieving $1&nbsp;billion in cost savings this year. We are continuing to strategically review
our portfolio over the next three months in an effort to ensure it drives growth and delivers value. Our team members, led by WBA&#146;s new executive committee with a track record of operational excellence, are powering our progress as we map
growth opportunities, aim to create long-term value across our businesses and execute the hard work to simplify and strengthen WBA.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:26%">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on
a forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort and the Company is unable to address the probable
significance of the unavailable information. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">&#147;Adjusted,&#148; &#147;constant currency&#148; and free cash flow
amounts are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. See the appendix to this release for a discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, including a reconciliation to the most closely
correlated GAAP measure. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Second Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA second quarter sales increased 6.3&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $37.1&nbsp;billion, an increase of
5.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting sales growth across all segments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second quarter operating loss was $13.2&nbsp;billion compared
to an operating income of $197&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Operating loss in the quarter includes a $12.4&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charge related to
VillageMD goodwill, which resulted in a $5.8&nbsp;billion charge attributable to WBA, net of tax and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-controlling</FONT> interest. Operating loss also reflects a $455&nbsp;million non-cash impairment charge
related to certain long-lived assets in the U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment. Adjusted operating income** was $900&nbsp;million, a decrease of 26.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis reflecting lower sale-leaseback gains and softer U.S. retail
performance, partly offset by improved profitability in the U.S. Healthcare segment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net loss in the second quarter was $5.9&nbsp;billion compared to net
earnings of $703&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges. Adjusted net earnings** increased 3.5&nbsp;percent to $1.0&nbsp;billion,
up 3.0&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, as lower adjusted operating income** was more than offset by the lower adjusted effective tax rate** compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter due to the recognition of
deferred tax assets in foreign jurisdictions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Loss per share in the second quarter was $6.85 compared to earnings per share of $0.81 in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted EPS** increased 3.4&nbsp;percent to $1.20, reflecting an increase of 2.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash used for operating activities was $637&nbsp;million in the second quarter. Operating cash flow was negatively impacted by $615&nbsp;million in
payments related to legal matters, a $379&nbsp;million Boots Pension Plan Annuity premium, and underlying seasonality. Year-over-year cash flow was negatively impacted by payments related to legal matters, phasing of working capital, and lower
earnings. Free cash flow** was negative $610&nbsp;million, a $1.3&nbsp;billion decrease compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Capital expenditures decreased by $146&nbsp;million compared to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fiscal 2024
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Year-to-Date</FONT></FONT> Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales in the first six months of fiscal 2024
increased 8.1&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period to $73.8&nbsp;billion, an increase of 7.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting growth across all segments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating loss in the first six months of fiscal 2024 was $13.2&nbsp;billion compared to an operating loss of $6.0&nbsp;billion in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Operating loss reflects a $12.4&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charge related to VillageMD goodwill, which resulted in a $5.8&nbsp;billion charge
attributable to WBA, net of tax and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-controlling</FONT> interest. Operating loss in the current period also reflects a $455&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charge related
to certain long-lived assets in the U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment. Prior year operating loss reflects a $6.8&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> charge for opioid-related claims and litigation. Adjusted operating income** was
$1.6&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 29.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis reflecting softer U.S. retail performance and lower sale-leaseback gains, partly offset by improved profitability in the U.S. Healthcare segment. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net loss for the first six months of fiscal 2024 was $6.0&nbsp;billion compared to net loss of
$3.0&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, reflecting the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges. Adjusted net earnings** decreased 19.8&nbsp;percent to $1.6&nbsp;billion, down
20.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower adjusted operating income** partly offset by a lower adjusted effective tax** rate due to the recognition of deferred tax assets in foreign jurisdictions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Loss per share for the first six months of fiscal 2024 was $6.93 compared to loss per share of $3.50 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
period. Adjusted EPS** decreased 19.9&nbsp;percent to $1.86, reflecting a decrease of 20.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash used for
operating activities was negative $918&nbsp;million in the first six months of fiscal 2024. Operating cash flow was negatively impacted by $699&nbsp;million in payments related to legal matters, a $379&nbsp;million Boots Pension Plan Annuity
premium, and underlying seasonality. Year-over-year cash flow was adversely impacted by phasing of working capital, lower earnings, and payments related to legal matters. Free cash flow** was negative $1.4&nbsp;billion, a $2.0&nbsp;billion decrease
compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Capital expenditures decreased by $250&nbsp;million compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment had second quarter sales of $28.9&nbsp;billion, an increase of 4.7&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable sales increased 4.8&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pharmacy sales increased 8.2&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable pharmacy sales increased
8.7&nbsp;percent in the quarter compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, benefiting from higher branded drug inflation and strong execution in pharmacy services. Comparable prescriptions filled in the second quarter,
adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents increased 2.7&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter while comparable prescriptions excluding immunizations increased 2.9&nbsp;percent.
Total prescriptions filled in the quarter, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents was 305.7&nbsp;million, an increase of 2.6&nbsp;percent versus the prior year quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail sales decreased 4.5&nbsp;percent and comparable retail sales decreased 4.3&nbsp;percent compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting a challenging retail environment, channel shift, and a weaker respiratory season, including a 170 basis point impact from lower seasonal and general merchandise sales, a 90 basis
point direct impact from softer cold cough flu trends, and a 40 basis point impact from adverse January weather. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted operating income** decreased
29.5&nbsp;percent to $752&nbsp;million compared to $1.1&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting lower retail sales, lower sale-leaseback gains, and higher shrink levels, partially offset by cost
savings compared to the prior year quarter. </P>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including a favorable currency impact of 3.4&nbsp;percent. Sales increased 3.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, with the Germany wholesale business growing 5.3&nbsp;percent and Boots UK

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Boots UK comparable retail sales increased 5.9&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter with growth across all categories, and increased total
retail market share. Boots.com continued to perform strongly with sales growing 16.8&nbsp;percent representing over 17&nbsp;percent of Boots total retail sales. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted operating income decreased 30.3&nbsp;percent to $245&nbsp;million, a decrease of 32.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, entirely due to lapping real estate gains in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Underlying growth offset inflationary pressures. </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The U.S. Healthcare segment had second quarter sales of $2.2&nbsp;billion, an increase of 33.2&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, aided by the acquisition of Summit Health by VillageMD. On a pro forma basis, the segment&#146;s businesses grew sales at a combined rate of 14&nbsp;percent in the quarter, led by VillageMD and
Shields. VillageMD grew 20&nbsp;percent on a pro forma basis, reflecting same clinic growth and additional full-risk lives under management. Shields grew 13&nbsp;percent, driven by recent contract wins and further expansion of existing partnerships.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating loss was $13.1&nbsp;billion, due to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charge related to VillageMD goodwill.
Adjusted operating loss**, which excludes impairment charges, stock compensation expense, and amortization of acquired intangible assets, was $34&nbsp;million compared to $159&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted EBITDA** of $17&nbsp;million improved by $127&nbsp;million versus the prior year quarter and represents the first quarter of positive
adjusted EBITDA** for the segment, driven by growth from VillageMD and Shields, and continued cost discipline. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">4 </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>We do not undertake, and expressly disclaim, any duty or obligation to update publicly any forward-looking statement after the date of this release,
whether as a result of new information, future events, changes in assumptions or otherwise. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Please refer to the supplemental information presented
below for reconciliations of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures used in this release to the most comparable GAAP financial measure and related disclosures. </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">ENDS </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Notes to Editors:
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots
Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is an integrated healthcare, pharmacy and retail leader serving millions of customers and patients every day, with a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">170-year</FONT> heritage of caring for communities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A trusted, global innovator in retail pharmacy with approximately 12,500 locations across the U.S., Europe and Latin America, WBA plays a critical role in the
healthcare ecosystem. The Company is reimagining local healthcare and well-being for all as part of its purpose &#150; to create more joyful lives through better health. Through dispensing medicines, improving access to a wide range of health
services, providing high quality health and beauty products and offering anytime, anywhere convenience across its digital platforms, WBA is shaping the future of healthcare. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA employs approximately 330,000 people and has a presence in eight countries through its portfolio of consumer brands: Walgreens, Boots, Duane Reade, the
No7 Beauty Company, and Benavides in Mexico. Additionally, WBA has a portfolio of healthcare-focused investments located in several countries, including China and the U.S. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA has been
recognized for its commitment to being an inclusive workplace. In fiscal 2023, the Company received a score of 100 from the Human Rights Campaign&#146;s Corporate Equality Index, scored 100&nbsp;percent on the Disability Equality Index for
disability inclusion and was named Disability:IN&#146;s 2023 Employer of the Year. In addition, WBA has been recognized for its commitment to operating sustainably as the company is an index component of the Dow Jones Sustainability Indices (DJSI).
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">More Company information is available at www.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following information provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under
the SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The Company has provided the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and
presented in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because
management has evaluated the Company&#146;s financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the Company from period to period and trends in the Company&#146;s historical
operating results. The Company also uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures as a basis for certain compensation programs it sponsors. These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial
measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates to the most directly comparable GAAP financial
measures on a forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of
forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet occurred, are out of the Company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, such as unusual <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> charges, tax expenses, and
material litigation expenses, and that would impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the Company is unable to address the probable significance of the
unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially from the corresponding GAAP financial measures.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company also presents certain
information related to current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the
foreign currency exchange rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The Company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the U.S. reporting in currencies other than the U.S.
dollar and such presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Comparable sales </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fiscal 2024 second-quarter comparable sales and prescriptions filled figures for the Company exclude the benefit of this year&#146;s leap day. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy and International segments, Comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at least
twelve consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster, in the past twelve months as well as <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. Comparable sales in constant currency exclude wholesale sales in Germany and sales from dispositions in the current period. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include
digitally initiated sales online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable sales for the first twelve months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first twelve months
after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT>
equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. The method of calculating comparable sales
varies across the retail industry and our method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same as other retailers&#146; methods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With respect to
the International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales, are presented on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion
above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company considers certain metrics, such as comparable sales (in constant currency), comparable pharmacy sales (in constant currency), comparable retail
sales (in constant currency), comparable number of prescriptions, comparable prescriptions excluding immunizations, and comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions to be key performance indicators because the
Company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the
Company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP
financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other companies. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, inventory
valuation adjustments and stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed
technology and contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The
revenue generated by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular
period unless an intangible asset becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements
of Earnings. The stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustment reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense
recognized in excess of the original grant date fair value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and
are not reflective of normal operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities recorded in Operating (loss) income within the Consolidated Condensed Statement of Earnings. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance, stock-based compensation, employee transaction success bonuses, and
other integration related exit and disposal charges. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs are significantly impacted by the
timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These
charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring
activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings in Cencora consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by Cencora consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if the U.S. Retail Pharmacy
segment inventory is accounted for using <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix,
and manufacturer pricing practices, which may be impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the Company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Impairment of goodwill, intangibles and long-lived assets recognized in the three months ended
February&nbsp;29, 2024 resulting from the interim goodwill impairment assessment for the VillageMD reporting unit. These charges do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating
operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded within Selling, general and
administrative expenses and Impairment of goodwill within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">7</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain
legal proceedings, including legal defense costs. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation
of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. In fiscal 2023, the Company recorded charges related to the opioid
litigation settlement frameworks and certain other legal matters. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because these do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

consist of the proportionate share of certain equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
adjustments. These charges are recorded in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Post-tax</FONT> earnings from other equity method investments within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and
board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method investments are not intended to imply that the Company has direct control over their operations and resulting
revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company reconciles Adjusted EBITDA for the U.S. Healthcare segment to Operating loss as the closest GAAP
measure for the segment profitability. The Company does not measure Net earnings attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. for its segments. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Impairment of goodwill, intangibles and long-lived assets recognized in the three months ended
February&nbsp;29, 2024 resulting from the interim goodwill impairment assessment for the VillageMD reporting unit. These charges do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating
operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded within Selling, general and
administrative expenses and Impairment of goodwill within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, inventory
valuation adjustments and stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed
technology and contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The
revenue generated by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular
period unless an intangible asset becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements
of Earnings. The stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustment reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense
recognized in excess of the original grant date fair value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and
are not reflective of normal operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities recorded in Operating (loss) income within the Consolidated Condensed Statement of Earnings. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance, stock-based compensation, employee transaction success bonuses, and
other integration related exit and disposal charges. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs are significantly impacted by the
timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These
charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring
activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Includes GAAP stock-based compensation expense excluding expenses related to acquisition-related amortization
and acquisition-related costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property,
plant and equipment (capital expenditures), plus acquisition related payments made in that period. This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for
debt service and other contractual obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to the Consolidated Condensed Statement of
Cash Flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the three months ended February&nbsp;28, 2023, the Company paid $335&nbsp;million to settle liability
classified share-based payment awards related to acquiring the remaining 30% equity interest in Shields. The Company also paid <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> compensation costs related to VillageMD&#146;s acquisition of Summit. The
payments are not indicative of normal operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the three-month period ending on February&nbsp;29, 2024, the Company made incremental pension
contributions of $379M to the Boots Plan as part of the Trustee&#146;s acquisition of a bulk annuity policy (the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Buy-In&#148;)</FONT> from Legal and General. The payments are not indicative of normal operating
performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">#&#8195;#&#8195;#&#8195;#&#8195;# </P>
